    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SOCKETS DO
    L_Rule_Active := FALSE;
    L_Rule_State := FALSE;
    
    L_Physical_Trig[L_i](CLK := VI_Physical_Switches[L_i]);
    L_Manual_Trig[L_i](CLK := VI_Manual_Override[L_i]);
    
    // Ручное переключение
    IF L_Physical_Trig[L_i].Q OR L_Manual_Trig[L_i].Q THEN
        L_Internal_State[L_i] := NOT L_Internal_State[L_i];
    END_IF;

    // Проверка правил для текущей групповой розетки помещения
    FOR L_j := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_RULES DO
        IF VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Active AND VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Target_ID = L_i THEN
            IF VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Action_Type = E_Rule_Action_Type.ACTION_SET_SOCKET THEN
                L_Rule_Active := TRUE;
                L_Rule_State := (VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Value > 0.5);
                L_Internal_State[L_i] := L_Rule_State; // Синхронизация внутреннего состояния
            ELSIF VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Action_Type = E_Rule_Action_Type.ACTION_TOGGLE_SOCKET AND VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Triggered THEN
                L_Internal_State[L_i] := NOT L_Internal_State[L_i]; // Toggle
            END_IF;
        END_IF;
    END_FOR;

    // Аварийное отключение
    IF VI_Fire_Alarm OR VI_Flood_Alarm THEN
        // Группы 1-4 неотключаемые (холодильник, сервер и т.д.)
        IF L_i > 4 THEN
            VO_Socket_States[L_i] := FALSE;
        ELSE
            // Критические розетки сохраняют свое текущее внутреннее состояние, а не форсируются в TRUE
            VO_Socket_States[L_i] := L_Internal_State[L_i];
        END_IF;
    ELSIF VI_Scenario = E_SCENARIO_TYPE.SCENARIO_AWAY OR VI_Security_Armed THEN
        // Master Off
        IF L_i > 4 THEN
            VO_Socket_States[L_i] := FALSE;
        ELSE
            // Неотключаемые группы розеток могут управляться вручную
            VO_Socket_States[L_i] := L_Internal_State[L_i];
        END_IF;
    ELSE
        // Нормальный режим: состояние определяется внутренним состоянием (ручным или правилом)
        IF L_Rule_Active THEN
            VO_Socket_States[L_i] := L_Rule_State;
        ELSE
            VO_Socket_States[L_i] := L_Internal_State[L_i];
        END_IF;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

VO_Internal_States := L_Internal_State;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_State_Manager
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT; // Системное время (мс)
    VI_IsActivePLC    : BOOL; // Флаг: Данный ПЛК является ведущим
    VI_Current_State  : ST_System_State_Summary; // Текущее сводное состояние системы
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Alarm_Active   : BOOL; // Глобальный флаг активной тревоги
    VO_Warning_Active : BOOL; // Глобальный флаг активного предупреждения
END_VAR

IF VI_IsActivePLC THEN
    VO_Alarm_Active := VI_Current_State.Gas_Alarm OR VI_Current_State.Fire_Alarm OR VI_Current_State.Flood_Alarm OR VI_Current_State.Security_Alarm;
    VO_Warning_Active := FALSE; // Добавить логику предупреждений
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_State_Replication
VAR_INPUT
    VI_Local_Role : E_PLC_ROLE; // Локальная роль ПЛК (Active/Standby)
    VI_Sync_Req : BOOL; // Запрос на принудительную синхронизацию
    VI_Local_State : ST_System_State_Snapshot; // Локальное состояние системы
    VI_Remote_State : ST_System_State_Snapshot; // Состояние системы партнера
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT; // Системное время (мс)
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_State_Updated : BOOL; // Флаг: Состояние было обновлено
    VO_Synced_State : ST_System_State_Snapshot; // Синхронизированное состояние
END_VAR
VAR
    L_Sync_In_Progress : BOOL;
    L_Last_Sync_Time : UDINT;
    L_Periodic_Sync_Req : BOOL;
    L_Elapsed_Time : UDINT;
END_VAR

// Периодическая синхронизация (каждые 5 секунд)
L_Elapsed_Time := F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Last_Sync_Time);

IF L_Elapsed_Time > 5000 THEN
    L_Periodic_Sync_Req := TRUE;
    L_Last_Sync_Time := VI_System_Time_MS;
ELSE
    L_Periodic_Sync_Req := FALSE;
END_IF;

// State Replication Logic
// Синхронизация состояния между ПЛК (ТЗ 8.2)
IF (VI_Sync_Req OR L_Periodic_Sync_Req) AND NOT L_Sync_In_Progress THEN
    L_Sync_In_Progress := TRUE;
    
    // Разрешение конфликтов на основе версии состояния
    IF VI_Remote_State.Version > VI_Local_State.Version THEN
        VO_Synced_State := VI_Remote_State;
        VO_State_Updated := TRUE;
    ELSIF VI_Remote_State.Version = VI_Local_State.Version THEN
        // Если версии равны, приоритет у ведущего ПЛК
        IF VI_Local_Role = E_PLC_ROLE.ROLE_STANDBY THEN
            VO_Synced_State := VI_Remote_State;
            VO_State_Updated := TRUE;
        ELSE
            VO_Synced_State := VI_Local_State;
            VO_State_Updated := FALSE;
        END_IF;
    ELSE
        VO_Synced_State := VI_Local_State;
        VO_State_Updated := FALSE;
    END_IF;
ELSIF NOT (VI_Sync_Req OR L_Periodic_Sync_Req) THEN
    L_Sync_In_Progress := FALSE;
    VO_State_Updated := FALSE;
    VO_Synced_State := VI_Local_State;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_State_Snapshot_Manager
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT;
    VI_Trigger_Event  : BOOL; // Сигнал на создание снимка
    VI_Event_Code     : WORD;
    VI_Current_State  : ST_State_Snapshot;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Snapshot_Saved : BOOL;
END_VAR
VAR
    L_Snapshot_Buffer : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_STATE_SNAPSHOTS] OF ST_State_Snapshot;
    L_Write_Idx       : INT := 1;
END_VAR

IF VI_Trigger_Event THEN
    L_Snapshot_Buffer[L_Write_Idx] := VI_Current_State;
    L_Snapshot_Buffer[L_Write_Idx].timestamp_ms := VI_System_Time_MS;
    L_Snapshot_Buffer[L_Write_Idx].trigger_event_code := VI_Event_Code;
    
    L_Write_Idx := (L_Write_Idx MOD GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_STATE_SNAPSHOTS) + 1;
    VO_Snapshot_Saved := TRUE;
ELSE
    VO_Snapshot_Saved := FALSE;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_State_Snapshot_NVRAM
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT;
    VI_Save_Req       : BOOL;
    VI_Snapshot       : ST_State_Snapshot;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Saved          : BOOL;
    VO_Error          : BOOL;
END_VAR
VAR
    L_FileName        : STRING := '/home/root/snapshot.bin';
    L_State           : INT := 0;
    
    // Асинхронные блоки из библиотеки CAA_File
    fbFileOpen        : FILE.Open;
    fbFileWrite       : FILE.Write;
    fbFileClose       : FILE.Close;
    L_FileHandle      : FILE.HANDLE;
END_VAR

CASE L_State OF
    0: // Ожидание
        VO_Saved := FALSE;
        VO_Error := FALSE;
        IF VI_Save_Req THEN
            L_State := 10;
            fbFileOpen(xExecute := FALSE);
            fbFileWrite(xExecute := FALSE);
            fbFileClose(xExecute := FALSE);
        END_IF;
        
    10: // Открытие файла
        fbFileOpen(
            xExecute := TRUE,
            sFileName := L_FileName,
            eFileMode := FILE.MODE.MWRITE
        );
        IF fbFileOpen.xDone THEN
            L_FileHandle := fbFileOpen.hFile;
            fbFileOpen(xExecute := FALSE);
            L_State := 20;
        ELSIF fbFileOpen.xError THEN
            VO_Error := TRUE;
            L_State := 0;
        END_IF;
        
    20: // Запись
        fbFileWrite(
            xExecute := TRUE,
            hFile := L_FileHandle,
            pBuffer := ADR(VI_Snapshot),
            szSize := SIZEOF(VI_Snapshot)
        );
        IF fbFileWrite.xDone THEN
            fbFileWrite(xExecute := FALSE);
            L_State := 30;
        ELSIF fbFileWrite.xError THEN
            VO_Error := TRUE;
            L_State := 30; // Все равно закрываем файл
        END_IF;
        
    30: // Закрытие
        fbFileClose(
            xExecute := TRUE,
            hFile := L_FileHandle
        );
        IF fbFileClose.xDone THEN
            fbFileClose(xExecute := FALSE);
            IF NOT VO_Error THEN
                VO_Saved := TRUE;
            END_IF;
            L_State := 0;
        ELSIF fbFileClose.xError THEN
            VO_Error := TRUE;
            L_State := 0;
        END_IF;
END_CASE;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Supply_Ventilation_Controller
VAR_INPUT
    VI_Outdoor_Temp : REAL;
    VI_Supply_Temp  : REAL; // Температура приточного воздуха
    VI_Target_Temp  : REAL;
    VI_Config       : ST_Ventilation_Unit_Config;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Heater_Power : REAL; // 0-100%
    VO_Fan_Speed    : BYTE; // 0-100%
END_VAR
VAR
    L_PID : FB_PID_Controller;
END_VAR

// ПИД-регулятор калорифера
L_PID(
    VI_SetPoint := VI_Target_Temp,
    VI_ProcessValue := VI_Supply_Temp, // Используем датчик притока
    VI_Kp := 5.0, VI_Tn := 60.0, VI_Tv := 0.0,
    VI_Y_Min := 0.0, VI_Y_Max := 100.0, VI_Cycle_Time_S := 1.0,
    VO_Output => VO_Heater_Power
);

VO_Fan_Speed := 50; // Базовая скорость

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
// ==============================================================================
// Блок таймера, привязанный к системному времени (System Timer)
// Назначение:
// - Замена стандартного TON для обеспечения точной выдержки времени,
//   независимой от времени цикла ПЛК, с использованием единого системного времени.
// ==============================================================================
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_System_Timer
VAR_INPUT
    IN : BOOL; // Вход запуска таймера
    PT : TIME; // Заданное время
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT; // Системное время (мс)
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    Q : BOOL; // Выход: таймер сработал
    ET : TIME; // Прошедшее время
END_VAR
VAR
    L_Start_Time : UDINT;
    L_Running : BOOL;
END_VAR

IF IN THEN
    IF NOT L_Running THEN
        L_Start_Time := VI_System_Time_MS;
        L_Running := TRUE;
        ET := T#0s;
        Q := FALSE;
    ELSE
        // Обработка переполнения UDINT (примерно 49 дней)
        ET := TO_TIME(F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Start_Time));
        
        IF ET >= PT THEN
            Q := TRUE;
            ET := PT;
        ELSE
            Q := FALSE;
        END_IF;
    END_IF;
ELSE
    L_Running := FALSE;
    ET := T#0s;
    Q := FALSE;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
// ==============================================================================
// Блок таймера задержки выключения (System Timer TOF)
// Назначение:
// - Замена стандартного TOF для обеспечения точной выдержки времени,
//   независимой от времени цикла ПЛК, с использованием единого системного времени.
// ==============================================================================
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_System_Timer_TOF
VAR_INPUT
    IN : BOOL; // Вход запуска таймера
    PT : TIME; // Заданное время
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT; // Системное время (мс)
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    Q : BOOL; // Выход: таймер сработал
    ET : TIME; // Прошедшее время
END_VAR
VAR
    L_Start_Time : UDINT;
    L_Running : BOOL;
    L_Prev_IN : BOOL;
END_VAR

IF IN THEN
    Q := TRUE;
    ET := T#0s;
    L_Running := FALSE;
ELSE
    IF L_Prev_IN THEN
        L_Start_Time := VI_System_Time_MS;
        L_Running := TRUE;
        ET := T#0s;
    END_IF;
    
    IF L_Running THEN
        // Обработка переполнения UDINT (примерно 49 дней)
        ET := TO_TIME(F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Start_Time));
        
        IF ET >= PT THEN
            Q := FALSE;
            ET := PT;
            L_Running := FALSE;
        ELSE
            Q := TRUE;
        END_IF;
    END_IF;
END_IF;

L_Prev_IN := IN;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Trend_Analyzer
VAR_INPUT
    VI_Data       : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_TREND_DATA_POINTS] OF REAL;
    VI_Count      : INT;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Average    : REAL;
    VO_Max        : REAL;
    VO_Min        : REAL;
    VO_Trend_Up   : BOOL;
    VO_Trend_Down : BOOL;
END_VAR
VAR
    L_i   : INT;
    L_Sum : REAL;
END_VAR

IF VI_Count > 0 AND VI_Count <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_TREND_DATA_POINTS THEN
    VO_Max := VI_Data[1];
    VO_Min := VI_Data[1];
    L_Sum := 0.0;
    
    FOR L_i := 1 TO VI_Count DO
        IF VI_Data[L_i] > VO_Max THEN VO_Max := VI_Data[L_i]; END_IF;
        IF VI_Data[L_i] < VO_Min THEN VO_Min := VI_Data[L_i]; END_IF;
        L_Sum := L_Sum + VI_Data[L_i];
    END_FOR;
    
    VO_Average := L_Sum / INT_TO_REAL(VI_Count);
    
    IF VI_Count >= 2 THEN
        VO_Trend_Up := (VI_Data[VI_Count] > VI_Data[1]);
        VO_Trend_Down := (VI_Data[VI_Count] < VI_Data[1]);
    END_IF;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Trend_Logger
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT;
    VI_Config : ST_Trend_Config;
    VI_Current_Value : REAL;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Data : ST_Trend_Data;
END_VAR
VAR
    L_Last_Log_Time : UDINT;
    L_Last_Value : REAL;
    L_Deviation : REAL;
END_VAR

IF NOT VI_Config.enabled THEN RETURN; END_IF;

// Логирование по изменению (Deadband) или по времени (раз в час)
L_Deviation := ABS(VI_Current_Value - L_Last_Value);
IF (L_Deviation >= (L_Last_Value * VI_Config.deviation_threshold_percent / 100.0)) OR 
   (F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Last_Log_Time) >= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MS_IN_HOUR) THEN
    
    // Запись в массив
    VO_Data.write_index := (VO_Data.record_count MOD 100) + 1;
    VO_Data.values[VO_Data.write_index] := VI_Current_Value;
    VO_Data.timestamps[VO_Data.write_index] := VI_System_Time_MS;

    VO_Data.record_count := VO_Data.record_count + 1;
    VO_Data.sum_values := VO_Data.sum_values + VI_Current_Value;
    
    L_Last_Value := VI_Current_Value;
    L_Last_Log_Time := VI_System_Time_MS;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_TwoFactor_Auth
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT;
    VI_Start_Auth     : BOOL;
    VI_Method         : E_TwoFactor_Method;
    VI_User_Code      : STRING(6);
    VI_Reset_Success  : BOOL; // Сброс успешного состояния
    VI_Shared_Secret  : STRING(32);
    VI_Max_Attempts   : BYTE := 3;
    VI_Timeout_MS     : UDINT := GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MS_IN_MINUTE * 5;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_State          : ST_TwoFactor_Auth_State;
    VO_Send_Code_Req  : BOOL; // Запрос на отправку кода (например, через шлюз)
    VO_Code_To_Send   : STRING(6); // Сгенерированный код для отправки
END_VAR
VAR
    L_Generated_Code  : STRING(6) := '';
    L_Start_Time      : UDINT;
    R_Trig_Start      : R_TRIG;
    L_Prev_User_Code  : STRING(6);
    L_Lockout_Start_Time : UDINT; // Время начала блокировки
    fbHMAC            : FB_HMAC_SHA1;
    L_Elapsed_Time    : UDINT;
    L_Time_Step       : UDINT;
    L_Message         : ARRAY[0..7] OF BYTE;
    L_Key             : ARRAY[0..63] OF BYTE;
    L_Key_Length      : INT;
    L_Offset          : INT;
    L_Truncated_Hash  : UDINT;
    L_i               : INT;
    L_Current_TOTP    : STRING(6);
    L_Prev_TOTP       : STRING(6);
    L_Code_Valid      : BOOL;
END_VAR

R_Trig_Start(CLK := VI_Start_Auth);

IF VI_Reset_Success THEN
    VO_State.Is_Success := FALSE;
END_IF;

IF R_Trig_Start.Q AND NOT VO_State.is_pending AND NOT VO_State.Is_Locked THEN
    VO_State.is_pending := TRUE;
    VO_State.Method := VI_Method;
    VO_State.start_time := VI_System_Time_MS;
    VO_State.timeout_ms := VI_Timeout_MS;
    L_Start_Time := VI_System_Time_MS;
    VO_State.Attempts_Left := VI_Max_Attempts;
    VO_State.Is_Success := FALSE;
    VO_State.Is_Locked := FALSE;
    L_Prev_User_Code := '';
    
    L_Key_Length := LEN(VI_Shared_Secret);
    IF L_Key_Length > 32 THEN
        L_Key_Length := 32;
    END_IF;
    FOR L_i := 0 TO 63 DO
        IF L_i < L_Key_Length THEN
            L_Key[L_i] := TO_BYTE(VI_Shared_Secret[L_i + 1]);
        ELSE
            L_Key[L_i] := 0;
        END_IF;
    END_FOR;
    
    L_Time_Step := VI_System_Time_MS / 30000;
    FOR L_i := 0 TO 7 DO
        L_Message[7 - L_i] := TO_BYTE(SHR(L_Time_Step, L_i * 8) AND 16#FF);
    END_FOR;
    fbHMAC(Key := L_Key, KeyLength := L_Key_Length, Message := L_Message, MessageLength := 8);
    L_Offset := TO_INT(fbHMAC.Hash[19] AND 16#0F);
    L_Truncated_Hash := (SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset] AND 16#7F), 24) OR SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+1] AND 16#FF), 16) OR SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+2] AND 16#FF), 8) OR TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+3] AND 16#FF));
    L_Generated_Code := UDINT_TO_STRING(L_Truncated_Hash MOD 1000000);
    WHILE LEN(L_Generated_Code) < 6 DO
        L_Generated_Code := CONCAT('0', L_Generated_Code);
    END_WHILE;
    
    IF VI_Method = E_TwoFactor_Method.TF_METHOD_TOTP THEN
        VO_Code_To_Send := '';
        VO_Send_Code_Req := FALSE;
    ELSIF VI_Method = E_TwoFactor_Method.TF_METHOD_NONE THEN
        VO_Code_To_Send := '';
        VO_Send_Code_Req := FALSE;
        VO_State.Is_Success := TRUE;
        VO_State.is_pending := FALSE;
    ELSE
        VO_Code_To_Send := L_Generated_Code;
        VO_Send_Code_Req := TRUE;
    END_IF;
ELSE
    VO_Send_Code_Req := FALSE;
END_IF;

IF VO_State.is_pending THEN
    L_Elapsed_Time := F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Start_Time);

    IF L_Elapsed_Time < VO_State.timeout_ms THEN
        VO_State.Time_Left_S := TO_UINT((VO_State.timeout_ms - L_Elapsed_Time) / 1000);
    ELSE
        VO_State.Time_Left_S := 0;
    END_IF;
    
    IF VI_User_Code <> '' AND VI_User_Code <> L_Prev_User_Code THEN
        L_Code_Valid := FALSE;
        L_Key_Length := LEN(VI_Shared_Secret);
        IF L_Key_Length > 32 THEN
            L_Key_Length := 32;
        END_IF;
        FOR L_i := 0 TO 63 DO
            IF L_i < L_Key_Length THEN
                L_Key[L_i] := TO_BYTE(VI_Shared_Secret[L_i + 1]);
            ELSE
                L_Key[L_i] := 0;
            END_IF;
        END_FOR;
        
        L_Time_Step := VI_System_Time_MS / 30000;
        
        // Проверка текущего шага
        FOR L_i := 0 TO 7 DO L_Message[7 - L_i] := TO_BYTE(SHR(L_Time_Step, L_i * 8) AND 16#FF); END_FOR;
        fbHMAC(Key := L_Key, KeyLength := L_Key_Length, Message := L_Message, MessageLength := 8);
        L_Offset := TO_INT(fbHMAC.Hash[19] AND 16#0F);
        L_Truncated_Hash := (SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset] AND 16#7F), 24) OR SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+1] AND 16#FF), 16) OR SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+2] AND 16#FF), 8) OR TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+3] AND 16#FF));
        L_Current_TOTP := UDINT_TO_STRING(L_Truncated_Hash MOD 1000000);
        WHILE LEN(L_Current_TOTP) < 6 DO L_Current_TOTP := CONCAT('0', L_Current_TOTP); END_WHILE;
        
        // Проверка предыдущего шага (для компенсации рассинхронизации)
        IF L_Time_Step > 0 THEN
            FOR L_i := 0 TO 7 DO L_Message[7 - L_i] := TO_BYTE(SHR(L_Time_Step - 1, L_i * 8) AND 16#FF); END_FOR;
            fbHMAC(Key := L_Key, KeyLength := L_Key_Length, Message := L_Message, MessageLength := 8);
            L_Offset := TO_INT(fbHMAC.Hash[19] AND 16#0F);
            L_Truncated_Hash := (SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset] AND 16#7F), 24) OR SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+1] AND 16#FF), 16) OR SHL(TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+2] AND 16#FF), 8) OR TO_UDINT(fbHMAC.Hash[L_Offset+3] AND 16#FF));
            L_Prev_TOTP := UDINT_TO_STRING(L_Truncated_Hash MOD 1000000);
            WHILE LEN(L_Prev_TOTP) < 6 DO L_Prev_TOTP := CONCAT('0', L_Prev_TOTP); END_WHILE;
        ELSE
            L_Prev_TOTP := L_Current_TOTP;
        END_IF;
        
        IF VI_Method = E_TwoFactor_Method.TF_METHOD_TOTP THEN
            IF VI_User_Code = L_Current_TOTP OR VI_User_Code = L_Prev_TOTP THEN
                L_Code_Valid := TRUE;
            END_IF;
        ELSIF VI_Method = E_TwoFactor_Method.TF_METHOD_RFID OR VI_Method = E_TwoFactor_Method.TF_METHOD_BOTH THEN
            IF VI_User_Code = L_Generated_Code OR VI_User_Code = L_Current_TOTP OR VI_User_Code = L_Prev_TOTP THEN
                L_Code_Valid := TRUE;
            END_IF;
        END_IF;
        
        IF L_Code_Valid THEN
            VO_State.Is_Success := TRUE;
            VO_State.is_pending := FALSE;
        ELSE
            IF VO_State.Attempts_Left > 0 THEN
                VO_State.Attempts_Left := VO_State.Attempts_Left - 1;
            END_IF;
            
            IF VO_State.Attempts_Left = 0 THEN
                VO_State.Is_Locked := TRUE;
                VO_State.is_pending := FALSE;
                L_Lockout_Start_Time := VI_System_Time_MS; // Блокировка на время таймаута
            END_IF;
        END_IF;
    END_IF;
    L_Prev_User_Code := VI_User_Code;
    
    IF L_Elapsed_Time > VO_State.timeout_ms THEN
        VO_State.is_pending := FALSE; // Таймаут
    END_IF;
END_IF;

IF VO_State.Is_Locked THEN
    IF F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Lockout_Start_Time) >= VO_State.timeout_ms THEN
        VO_State.Is_Locked := FALSE;
    END_IF;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Valve_Test
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT;
    VI_Start_Test     : BOOL;
    VI_Valve_ID       : BYTE;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Test_Active    : BOOL;
    VO_Result         : E_Valve_Test_Result;
    VO_Valve_Cmd      : BOOL;
END_VAR
VAR
    L_Start_Time      : UDINT;
    L_State           : INT;
END_VAR

CASE L_State OF
    0: // Ожидание
        IF VI_Start_Test THEN
            VO_Test_Active := TRUE;
            VO_Result := E_Valve_Test_Result.TEST_RESULT_IN_PROGRESS;
            L_Start_Time := VI_System_Time_MS;
            VO_Valve_Cmd := TRUE; // Открыть
            L_State := 1;
        END_IF;
    1: // Тест
        IF F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Start_Time) > 5000 THEN
            VO_Valve_Cmd := FALSE; // Закрыть
            VO_Result := E_Valve_Test_Result.TEST_RESULT_PASSED; // Заглушка, нужен контроль концевиков
            VO_Test_Active := FALSE;
            L_State := 0;
        END_IF;
END_CASE;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Valve_Test_Manager
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT;
    VI_IsActivePLC : BOOL;
    VI_Valve_Currents : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS] OF REAL;
    VI_Valve_End_Switches : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS] OF BOOL;
    VI_Config : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS] OF ST_Valve_Test_Config;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Test_Active : BOOL;
    VO_Valve_Cmd : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS] OF BOOL;
    VO_Test_Results : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS] OF BOOL; // TRUE = OK
    VO_Status_Msg : STRING(200);
END_VAR
VAR
    L_State : INT;
    L_Current_Valve : INT := 1;
    L_Test_Start_Time : UDINT;
    L_Last_Test_Time : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS] OF UDINT;
    L_i : INT;
    L_Need_Test : BOOL;
    L_Elapsed_Time : UDINT;
END_VAR

IF NOT VI_IsActivePLC THEN RETURN; END_IF;

CASE L_State OF
    0: // Ожидание
        VO_Test_Active := FALSE;
        L_Need_Test := FALSE;
        
        // Поиск клапана, которому нужен тест (раз в неделю)
        FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS DO
            IF VI_Config[L_i].enabled AND (F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Last_Test_Time[L_i]) > (VI_Config[L_i].test_interval_days * 86400000)) THEN
                L_Current_Valve := L_i;
                L_Need_Test := TRUE;
                EXIT;
            END_IF;
        END_FOR;
        
        IF L_Need_Test THEN
            L_State := 1;
            L_Test_Start_Time := VI_System_Time_MS;
            VO_Test_Active := TRUE;
            VO_Valve_Cmd[L_Current_Valve] := TRUE; // Открываем
            VO_Status_Msg := CONCAT('ТЕСТ КЛАПАНА ', INT_TO_STRING(L_Current_Valve));
            VO_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve] := TRUE; // Сброс результата
        END_IF;
        
    1: // Тестирование (ожидание открытия)
        L_Elapsed_Time := F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Test_Start_Time);
        
        IF VI_Valve_End_Switches[L_Current_Valve] THEN
            // Концевик сработал до истечения таймаута
            // Проверка тока
            IF ABS(VI_Valve_Currents[L_Current_Valve] - VI_Config[L_Current_Valve].Nominal_Current) > (VI_Config[L_Current_Valve].Nominal_Current * 0.2) THEN
                VO_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve] := FALSE; // Ошибка по току
            END_IF;
            
            GVL_Retain.G_Valve_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve] := VO_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve];
            
            VO_Valve_Cmd[L_Current_Valve] := FALSE; // Закрываем
            L_Test_Start_Time := VI_System_Time_MS; // Перезапускаем таймер для проверки закрытия
            L_State := 2;
        ELSIF L_Elapsed_Time > TO_UDINT(VI_Config[L_Current_Valve].nominal_close_time_sec * 1000.0) THEN
            // Таймаут открытия (заклинивание)
            VO_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve] := FALSE; 
            GVL_Retain.G_Valve_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve] := FALSE;
            VO_Status_Msg := CONCAT('ОШИБКА: ЗАКЛИНИВАНИЕ КЛАПАНА ', INT_TO_STRING(L_Current_Valve));
            
            VO_Valve_Cmd[L_Current_Valve] := FALSE; // Закрываем
            L_Test_Start_Time := VI_System_Time_MS; // Перезапускаем таймер
            L_State := 2;
        END_IF;
        
    2: // Ожидание закрытия
        L_Elapsed_Time := F_TimeDiff(VI_System_Time_MS, L_Test_Start_Time);
        
        IF NOT VI_Valve_End_Switches[L_Current_Valve] THEN
            // Концевик разомкнулся (клапан закрыт)
            L_Last_Test_Time[L_Current_Valve] := VI_System_Time_MS;
            L_State := 0;
            IF VO_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve] THEN
                VO_Status_Msg := 'ТЕСТ ЗАВЕРШЕН УСПЕШНО';
            END_IF;
        ELSIF L_Elapsed_Time > TO_UDINT(VI_Config[L_Current_Valve].nominal_close_time_sec * 1000.0) THEN
            // Таймаут закрытия (заклинивание)
            VO_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve] := FALSE; 
            GVL_Retain.G_Valve_Test_Results[L_Current_Valve] := FALSE;
            VO_Status_Msg := CONCAT('ОШИБКА: НЕ ЗАКРЫЛСЯ КЛАПАН ', INT_TO_STRING(L_Current_Valve));
            
            L_Last_Test_Time[L_Current_Valve] := VI_System_Time_MS;
            L_State := 0;
        END_IF;
END_CASE;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Ventilation_System_Manager
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT; // Системное время (мс)
    VI_IsActivePLC : BOOL; // Флаг: Данный ПЛК является ведущим
    VI_Outdoor_Temp : REAL; // Уличная температура воздуха (°C)
    VI_Supply_Temps : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_TEMPS] OF REAL; // Температура приточного воздуха после калорифера
    VI_Room_Temps : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES] OF REAL; // Температура в помещениях (°C)
    VI_Room_Humidities : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_HUMIDITY_SENSORS] OF REAL; // Влажность в мокрых зонах (%)
    VI_Room_CO2 : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES] OF REAL; // Уровень CO2 в помещениях (ppm)
    VI_Current_Scenario : E_SCENARIO_TYPE; // Текущий глобальный сценарий
    VI_Config : ST_Ventilation_Global_Config; // Конфигурация системы вентиляции
    VI_Fire_Alarm : BOOL; // Сигнал пожарной тревоги
    VI_Gas_Alarm : BOOL; // Сигнал газовой тревоги
    VI_PV3_Boost_Req : BOOL; // Запрос форсирования ПВ-3 от газоанализатора (ТЗ 5.1)
    VI_Supply_100_Req : BOOL; // Запрос 100% притока (ТЗ 6.4)
    VI_Exhaust_100_Req : BOOL; // Запрос 100% вытяжки (ТЗ 6.4)
    VI_Supply_80_Req : BOOL; // Запрос 80% притока (ТЗ 5.4)
    VI_Vent_Stop : BOOL; // Запрос на остановку вентиляции (ТЗ 5.3)
    VI_Wet_Zone_Active : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_WET_ZONES] OF BOOL; // Сигналы включения света в санузлах (ТЗ 4.0)
    VI_Rule_Actions : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_RULES] OF ST_Rule_Action; // Действия от Rule Engine
    VI_IO_Modules_Online : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MODULES] OF BOOL; // Статусы модулей ввода-вывода
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Supply_Fans : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_FANS] OF BYTE; // Выход: Управление приточными вентиляторами (0-100%)
    VO_Exhaust_Fans : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_EXHAUST_FANS] OF BYTE; // Выход: Управление вытяжными вентиляторами (0-100%)
    VO_Heater_Power : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS] OF REAL; // Выход: Мощность калориферов (0-100%)
    VO_Status_Msg : STRING(200); // Строковое сообщение о статусе
END_VAR
VAR
    L_i : INT;
    L_j : INT;
    L_Max_CO2 : REAL;
    L_Max_Hum : REAL;
    L_Base_Speed : BYTE;
    L_Target_Temp : REAL;
    L_PID_Heaters : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS] OF FB_PID_Controller;
    L_Wet_Zone_Timers : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_WET_ZONES] OF FB_System_Timer_TOF; // Таймеры выбега для вытяжек санузлов
END_VAR

// Проверка связи с модулями ввода-вывода
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MODULES DO
    IF NOT VI_IO_Modules_Online[L_i] THEN
        // Переход в безопасное состояние при потере связи (отключение вентиляции)
        FOR L_j := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_FANS DO VO_Supply_Fans[L_j] := 0; END_FOR;
        FOR L_j := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_EXHAUST_FANS DO VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_j] := 0; END_FOR;
        FOR L_j := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS DO VO_Heater_Power[L_j] := 0.0; END_FOR;
        VO_Status_Msg := 'ОШИБКА: Потеря связи с модулями ввода-вывода';
        RETURN;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

// 1. Определение базовой скорости и целевой температуры по сценарию (ТЗ 7.1)
CASE VI_Current_Scenario OF
    E_SCENARIO_TYPE.SCENARIO_AWAY:
        L_Base_Speed := VI_Config.Scenario_Modes[3].Base_Fan_Speed;
        L_Target_Temp := VI_Config.Scenario_Modes[3].Target_Temp;
    E_SCENARIO_TYPE.SCENARIO_SLEEP:
        L_Base_Speed := VI_Config.Scenario_Modes[2].Base_Fan_Speed;
        L_Target_Temp := VI_Config.Scenario_Modes[2].Target_Temp;
    ELSE // PRESENCE, MORNING, EVENING
        L_Base_Speed := VI_Config.Scenario_Modes[1].Base_Fan_Speed;
        L_Target_Temp := VI_Config.Scenario_Modes[1].Target_Temp;
END_CASE;

// 2. Логика управления приточными установками (П-1, П-2, П-3)
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_FANS DO
    // ПИД-регулирование мощности электрического калорифера
    IF L_i <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_TEMPS THEN
        L_PID_Heaters[L_i](
            VI_SetPoint := L_Target_Temp,
            VI_ProcessValue := VI_Supply_Temps[L_i], // Используем датчик температуры после калорифера
            VI_Kp := 4.0, VI_Tn := 120.0, VI_Tv := 0.0,
            VI_Y_Min := 0.0, VI_Y_Max := 100.0, VI_Cycle_Time_S := 1.0,
            VO_Output => VO_Heater_Power[L_i]
        );
    END_IF;

    // Определение скорости приточного вентилятора
    VO_Supply_Fans[L_i] := L_Base_Speed;
    
    // Обработка действий от Rule Engine
    FOR L_j := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_RULES DO
        IF VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Active AND VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Target_ID = L_i THEN
            IF VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Action_Type = E_Rule_Action_Type.ACTION_SET_VENTILATION THEN
                VO_Supply_Fans[L_i] := REAL_TO_BYTE(VI_Rule_Actions[L_j].Value);
            END_IF;
        END_IF;
    END_FOR;
    
    // Обработка аварийных запросов (ТЗ 5.4, 6.4)
    IF VI_Supply_100_Req THEN
        VO_Supply_Fans[L_i] := 100;
        IF L_i <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_TEMPS THEN VO_Heater_Power[L_i] := 0.0; END_IF; // Отключение нагрева при аварийном проветривании
    ELSIF VI_Supply_80_Req THEN
        VO_Supply_Fans[L_i] := 80;
    END_IF;
    
    // Отключение при пожаре (ТЗ 5.3)
    IF VI_Fire_Alarm OR VI_Vent_Stop THEN
        VO_Supply_Fans[L_i] := 0;
        IF L_i <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_TEMPS THEN VO_Heater_Power[L_i] := 0.0; END_IF;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

// 3. Логика управления вытяжными установками (В-1 .. В-5)
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_EXHAUST_FANS DO
    VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := L_Base_Speed;
    
    // ТЗ 4.0: Логика вытяжки в санузлах
    FOR L_j := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_WET_ZONES DO
        IF VI_Config.wet_zone_to_exhaust_map[L_j] = L_i THEN
            // Включение по свету, выключение с задержкой 5 минут (используем TOF)
            L_Wet_Zone_Timers[L_j](IN := VI_Wet_Zone_Active[L_j], PT := T#5m, VI_System_Time_MS := VI_System_Time_MS);
            IF VI_Wet_Zone_Active[L_j] THEN
                VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := 80; // Повышенная скорость при присутствии
            ELSIF L_Wet_Zone_Timers[L_j].Q THEN
                VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := 50; // Скорость выбега (пока таймер TOF активен)
            END_IF;
        END_IF;
    END_FOR;

    // ТЗ 5.1: Форсирование ПВ-3 при утечке метана
    IF L_i = VI_Config.pv3_exhaust_index AND VI_PV3_Boost_Req THEN
        VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := 100;
    END_IF;

    // Обработка аварийных запросов (ТЗ 6.4)
    IF VI_Exhaust_100_Req THEN
        VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := 100;
    END_IF;
    
    // Отключение при пожаре (ТЗ 5.3)
    IF VI_Fire_Alarm OR VI_Vent_Stop THEN
        VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := 0;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

// 4. Формирование статусного сообщения
IF VI_Fire_Alarm THEN
    VO_Status_Msg := 'ВЕНТИЛЯЦИЯ: АВАРИЙНЫЙ РЕЖИМ (ПОЖАР)';
ELSIF VI_Gas_Alarm THEN
    VO_Status_Msg := 'ВЕНТИЛЯЦИЯ: АВАРИЙНОЕ ПРОВЕТРИВАНИЕ (ГАЗ)';
ELSE
    VO_Status_Msg := 'Вентиляция работает в штатном режиме';
END_IF;

// Если ПЛК в резерве, обнуляем выходы
IF NOT VI_IsActivePLC THEN
    FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_FANS DO 
        VO_Supply_Fans[L_i] := 0; 
        IF L_i <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_TEMPS THEN VO_Heater_Power[L_i] := 0.0; END_IF;
    END_FOR;
    FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_EXHAUST_FANS DO VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := 0; END_FOR;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Water_Leakage_Manager
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT; // Системное время (мс)
    VI_IsActivePLC    : BOOL; // Флаг: Данный ПЛК является ведущим
    VI_Sensors        : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_FLOOD_SENSORS] OF BOOL; // Сигналы от датчиков протечки (TRUE = протечка)
    VI_Config         : ST_Flood_Global_Config; // Конфигурация системы защиты от протечек
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Alarm_Active   : BOOL; // Глобальный флаг тревоги протечки
    VO_Warning_Active : BOOL; // Флаг предупреждения (протечка обнаружена, но клапаны еще не перекрыты)
    VO_Close_Valve_35 : BOOL; // Команда на закрытие клапана 35 (ХВС)
    VO_Close_Valve_36 : BOOL; // Команда на закрытие клапана 36 (ГВС)
    VO_Status_Msg     : STRING(200); // Строковое сообщение о статусе
END_VAR
VAR
    L_i               : INT;
    L_Sensor_Timers   : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_FLOOD_SENSORS] OF FB_System_Timer;
    L_Any_Leak        : BOOL;
    L_Any_Warning     : BOOL;
END_VAR

IF NOT VI_IsActivePLC THEN RETURN; END_IF;

L_Any_Leak := FALSE;
L_Any_Warning := FALSE;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_FLOOD_SENSORS DO
    L_Sensor_Timers[L_i](IN := VI_Sensors[L_i], PT := TO_TIME(VI_Config.min_duration_ms + VI_Config.warning_duration_ms), VI_System_Time_MS := VI_System_Time_MS);
    
    IF L_Sensor_Timers[L_i].ET >= TO_TIME(VI_Config.min_duration_ms) THEN
        L_Any_Warning := TRUE;
        
        // Двухступенчатая логика: перекрытие после warning_duration_ms
        IF L_Sensor_Timers[L_i].Q THEN
            L_Any_Leak := TRUE;
            IF VI_Config.sensor_to_valve_map[L_i] = 1 THEN
                VO_Close_Valve_35 := TRUE;
            ELSIF VI_Config.sensor_to_valve_map[L_i] = 2 THEN
                VO_Close_Valve_36 := TRUE;
            END_IF;
        END_IF;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

VO_Alarm_Active := L_Any_Leak;
VO_Warning_Active := L_Any_Warning;

IF VO_Alarm_Active THEN
    VO_Status_Msg := 'АВАРИЯ: ПРОТЕЧКА ВОДЫ. КЛАПАНЫ ЗАКРЫТЫ.';
ELSIF VO_Warning_Active THEN
    VO_Status_Msg := 'ПРЕДУПРЕЖДЕНИЕ: ОБНАРУЖЕНА ВОДА. ОЖИДАНИЕ ПЕРЕКРЫТИЯ.';
ELSE
    VO_Status_Msg := 'Система контроля протечек в норме';
    VO_Close_Valve_35 := FALSE;
    VO_Close_Valve_36 := FALSE;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Water_Valve_Controller IMPLEMENTS IValveController
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time : UDINT;
    VI_IsActivePLC : BOOL;
    VI_Flood_Alarm : BOOL;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Valve_Closed : BOOL;
    VO_Status_Msg   : STRING(200);
END_VAR

IF VI_Flood_Alarm AND VI_IsActivePLC THEN
    VO_Valve_Closed := TRUE;
    VO_Status_Msg := 'КЛАПАН ЗАКРЫТ ПО ПРОТЕЧКЕ';
END_IF;

METHOD OpenValve : BOOL
VAR_INPUT
    VI_Operator_ID : STRING(10);
    VI_Force : BOOL;
END_VAR
IF VI_IsActivePLC OR VI_Force THEN
    VO_Valve_Closed := FALSE;
    OpenValve := TRUE;
END_IF;
END_METHOD

METHOD CloseValve : BOOL
VAR_INPUT
    VI_Operator_ID : STRING(10);
    VI_Force : BOOL;
END_VAR
VO_Valve_Closed := TRUE;
CloseValve := TRUE;
END_METHOD

METHOD GetStatus : BYTE
GetStatus := TO_BYTE(SEL(VO_Valve_Closed, 0, 1));
END_METHOD

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Zone_Access_Manager
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT; // Системное время (мс)
    VI_Operator_ID    : STRING(10); // Идентификатор оператора
    VI_Target_Zone    : INT; // Номер целевой зоны
    VI_Rights         : ST_Operator_Zone_Rights; // Права доступа оператора к зоне
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Access_Granted : BOOL; // Флаг: Доступ разрешен
END_VAR

// Проверка прав доступа к зоне
IF VI_Target_Zone >= 1 AND VI_Target_Zone <= 32 THEN
    // Если глобальный уровень доступа высокий (например, CONFIG или FULL), разрешаем доступ ко всем зонам
    IF VI_Rights.global_access_level >= TO_BYTE(E_Zone_Access_Level.ZONE_ACCESS_CONFIG) THEN
        VO_Access_Granted := TRUE;
    ELSE
        // Иначе проверяем битовую маску для конкретной зоны
        // Бит 0 соответствует зоне 1, бит 1 - зоне 2 и т.д.
        VO_Access_Granted := (VI_Rights.zone_masks AND SHL(DWORD#1, VI_Target_Zone - 1)) <> 0;
    END_IF;
ELSE
    VO_Access_Granted := FALSE;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION F_TimeDiff : UDINT
VAR_INPUT
    VI_Current_Time : UDINT;
    VI_Previous_Time : UDINT;
END_VAR
// Безопасное вычисление разницы времени с учетом переполнения 32-битного таймера (UDINT)
IF VI_Current_Time >= VI_Previous_Time THEN
    F_TimeDiff := VI_Current_Time - VI_Previous_Time;
ELSE
    F_TimeDiff := (4294967295 - VI_Previous_Time) + VI_Current_Time + 1;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
INTERFACE IValveController
METHOD OpenValve : BOOL
VAR_INPUT
    VI_Operator_ID : STRING(10);
    VI_Force : BOOL;
END_VAR
END_METHOD

METHOD CloseValve : BOOL
VAR_INPUT
    VI_Operator_ID : STRING(10);
    VI_Force : BOOL;
END_VAR
END_METHOD

METHOD GetStatus : BYTE
END_METHOD

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_Interface_Contract_Validator
VAR_INPUT
    VI_System_Time_MS : UDINT;
    VI_Enable : BOOL;
    VI_Strict_Mode : BOOL;
    VI_Manifold_Valves : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS] OF REAL;
    VI_Boiler_Setpoints : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS] OF REAL;
    VI_Supply_Fans : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_FANS] OF BYTE;
    VI_Exhaust_Fans : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_EXHAUST_FANS] OF BYTE;
    VI_Lighting_Levels : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES] OF BYTE;
    VI_Blinds_Positions : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BLINDS] OF BYTE;
    VI_DALI_Zone_Map : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES] OF UINT;
    VI_KNX_Blinds_Map : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BLINDS] OF UINT;
END_VAR
VAR_OUTPUT
    VO_Manifold_Valves : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS] OF REAL;
    VO_Boiler_Setpoints : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS] OF REAL;
    VO_Supply_Fans : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_FANS] OF BYTE;
    VO_Exhaust_Fans : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_EXHAUST_FANS] OF BYTE;
    VO_Lighting_Levels : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES] OF BYTE;
    VO_Blinds_Positions : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BLINDS] OF BYTE;
    VO_Status : ST_Hardware_Integration_Status;
END_VAR
VAR
    L_i : INT;
END_VAR

VO_Status := (output_contract_ok := TRUE, lighting_contract_ok := TRUE, blinds_contract_ok := TRUE, vent_contract_ok := TRUE, heating_contract_ok := TRUE, last_error_code := 0, last_error_text := '', last_update_ms := VI_System_Time_MS);

IF NOT VI_Enable THEN
    VO_Manifold_Valves := VI_Manifold_Valves;
    VO_Boiler_Setpoints := VI_Boiler_Setpoints;
    VO_Supply_Fans := VI_Supply_Fans;
    VO_Exhaust_Fans := VI_Exhaust_Fans;
    VO_Lighting_Levels := VI_Lighting_Levels;
    VO_Blinds_Positions := VI_Blinds_Positions;
    RETURN;
END_IF;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS DO
    VO_Manifold_Valves[L_i] := LIMIT(0.0, VI_Manifold_Valves[L_i], 100.0);
    IF VO_Manifold_Valves[L_i] <> VI_Manifold_Valves[L_i] THEN
        VO_Status.heating_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.output_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.last_error_code := 16#E301;
        VO_Status.last_error_text := 'Heating valve command out of range';
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS DO
    VO_Boiler_Setpoints[L_i] := LIMIT(0.0, VI_Boiler_Setpoints[L_i], 100.0);
    IF VO_Boiler_Setpoints[L_i] <> VI_Boiler_Setpoints[L_i] THEN
        VO_Status.heating_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.output_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.last_error_code := 16#E302;
        VO_Status.last_error_text := 'Boiler setpoint out of range';
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_FANS DO
    VO_Supply_Fans[L_i] := LIMIT(TO_BYTE(0), VI_Supply_Fans[L_i], TO_BYTE(100));
    IF VO_Supply_Fans[L_i] <> VI_Supply_Fans[L_i] THEN
        VO_Status.vent_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.output_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.last_error_code := 16#E303;
        VO_Status.last_error_text := 'Supply fan command out of range';
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_EXHAUST_FANS DO
    VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := LIMIT(TO_BYTE(0), VI_Exhaust_Fans[L_i], TO_BYTE(100));
    IF VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] <> VI_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] THEN
        VO_Status.vent_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.output_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.last_error_code := 16#E304;
        VO_Status.last_error_text := 'Exhaust fan command out of range';
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES DO
    VO_Lighting_Levels[L_i] := LIMIT(TO_BYTE(0), VI_Lighting_Levels[L_i], TO_BYTE(100));
    IF VO_Lighting_Levels[L_i] <> VI_Lighting_Levels[L_i] THEN
        VO_Status.lighting_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.output_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.last_error_code := 16#E305;
        VO_Status.last_error_text := 'Lighting level out of range';
    END_IF;
    IF VI_Strict_Mode AND VI_DALI_Zone_Map[L_i] = 0 THEN
        VO_Status.lighting_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.output_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.last_error_code := 16#E306;
        VO_Status.last_error_text := 'Missing DALI zone map';
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BLINDS DO
    VO_Blinds_Positions[L_i] := LIMIT(TO_BYTE(0), VI_Blinds_Positions[L_i], TO_BYTE(100));
    IF VO_Blinds_Positions[L_i] <> VI_Blinds_Positions[L_i] THEN
        VO_Status.blinds_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.output_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.last_error_code := 16#E307;
        VO_Status.last_error_text := 'Blinds position out of range';
    END_IF;
    IF VI_Strict_Mode AND VI_KNX_Blinds_Map[L_i] = 0 THEN
        VO_Status.blinds_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.output_contract_ok := FALSE;
        VO_Status.last_error_code := 16#E308;
        VO_Status.last_error_text := 'Missing KNX blinds map';
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
PROGRAM MAIN
VAR
END_VAR

// Вызов основных программ
PRG_IO_Read();
PRG_System();
PRG_Safety();
PRG_Security();
PRG_Heating();
PRG_Ventilation();
PRG_Lighting();
PRG_IO_Write();

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
PROGRAM PRG_Heating
VAR
    fbDHWManager : FB_DHW_Manager;
    fbHeatingManager : FB_Heating_System_Manager;
    fbValveTestManager : FB_Valve_Test_Manager;
    L_i : INT;
END_VAR

// 12. Управление ГВС
fbDHWManager(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Current_TOD := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_TOD,
    VI_IsActivePLC := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC,
    VI_Temp := GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Temp,
    VI_Pressure := GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Pressure,
    VI_Config := GVL_CONFIG.G_DHW_Config,
    VI_Current_Day_Of_Week := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Day,
    VI_IO_Modules_Online := GVL_STATUS.G_IO_Modules_Online,
    VI_Reset_Errors := GVL_COMMAND.G_Reset_Errors,
    VO_Heating_Pump => GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Heating_Pump,
    VO_Circ_Pump => GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Circ_Pump,
    VO_Status => GVL_STATUS.G_DHW_Status
);

// 9. Управление климатом (Отопление)
fbHeatingManager(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Current_TOD := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_TOD,
    VI_IsActivePLC := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC,
    VI_Outdoor_Temp := GVL_STATE.G_Outdoor_Temp,
    VI_Floor_Temps := GVL_STATE.G_Floor_Temps,
    VI_Room_Temps := GVL_STATE.G_Room_Temps,
    VI_Config := GVL_CONFIG.G_Heating_Config,
    VI_Zone_Configs := GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_FloorHeating_Configs,
    VI_Tariff := GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Tariff_Settings,
    VI_Current_Hour := TO_UINT(GVL_STATUS.G_Time_Of_Day_MS / GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MS_IN_HOUR),
    VI_Manifold_Pressures := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pressures,
    VI_Manifold_Currents := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Currents,
    VI_Manifold_Temps_Supply := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_T_Supply,
    VI_Manifold_Temps_Return := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_T_Return,
    VI_Boiler_Flame_Status := GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Flame,
    VI_Rule_Actions := GVL_STATE.G_Rule_Actions,
    VI_Boiler_Stop := GVL_COMMAND.G_Boiler_Stop,
    VI_IO_Modules_Online := GVL_STATUS.G_IO_Modules_Online,
    VI_DHW_Heating_Demand := GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Heating_Pump,
    VI_DHW_Target_Temp := GVL_CONFIG.G_DHW_Config.Target_Temp,
    VI_Current_Scenario := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario,
    VI_Scenario_Configs := GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Scenario_Configs,
    VO_Manifold_Valves => GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Valves,
    VO_Manifold_Pumps => GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pumps,
    VO_Zone_Valves => GVL_STATE.G_Zone_Valves,
    VO_Boiler_Enable => GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Enable,
    VO_Boiler_Setpoint => GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Setpoint,
    VO_Status => GVL_STATUS.G_Manifold_Status,
    VO_Boiler_Status => GVL_STATUS.G_Boiler_Status
);

// 11.5. Тестирование клапанов
fbValveTestManager(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_IsActivePLC := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC,
    VI_Valve_Currents := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Currents,
    VI_Valve_End_Switches := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_End_Switches,
    VI_Config := GVL_CONFIG.G_Valve_Test_Config
);

IF fbValveTestManager.VO_Test_Active THEN
    FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS DO
        IF fbValveTestManager.VO_Valve_Cmd[L_i] THEN
            GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Valves[L_i] := 100.0;
        ELSE
            GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Valves[L_i] := 0.0;
        END_IF;
    END_FOR;
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
PROGRAM PRG_IO_Read
VAR
    L_i : INT;
    L_Debounce_Time : TIME := T#100MS;
    
    fbDebounce_Switches : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES] OF FB_System_Timer;
    fbDebounce_Socket_Switches : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SOCKETS] OF FB_System_Timer;
    fbDebounce_Motion : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES] OF FB_System_Timer;
    fbDebounce_Security_Open : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SECURITY_SENSORS] OF FB_System_Timer;
    fbDebounce_Security_Glass : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SECURITY_SENSORS] OF FB_System_Timer;
    fbDebounce_Flood : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_FLOOD_SENSORS] OF FB_System_Timer;
    fbDebounce_Smoke : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SMOKE_SENSORS] OF FB_System_Timer;
    fbDebounce_Group_2F : FB_System_Timer;
    
    fbIO_Watchdog_1 : FB_IO_Module_Watchdog;
    fbIO_Watchdog_2 : FB_IO_Module_Watchdog;
    L_IO_Error_Active : BOOL;
END_VAR

// 0. КОНТРОЛЬ СВЯЗИ С МОДУЛЯМИ ВВОДА-ВЫВОДА (Watchdog)
fbIO_Watchdog_1(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Module_ID := 1,
    VI_Heartbeat_Signal := GVL_IO.DI_Module_1_Heartbeat,
    VI_Timeout_MS := 2000
);

fbIO_Watchdog_2(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Module_ID := 2,
    VI_Heartbeat_Signal := GVL_IO.DI_Module_2_Heartbeat,
    VI_Timeout_MS := 2000
);

GVL_STATUS.G_IO_Modules_Online[1] := fbIO_Watchdog_1.VO_Module_Online;
GVL_STATUS.G_IO_Modules_Online[2] := fbIO_Watchdog_2.VO_Module_Online;

L_IO_Error_Active := fbIO_Watchdog_1.VO_Error_Active OR fbIO_Watchdog_2.VO_Error_Active;

IF L_IO_Error_Active THEN
    GVL_COMMAND.G_Gas_Valve_Close := TRUE;
    GVL_COMMAND.G_Close_Valve_35 := TRUE;
    GVL_COMMAND.G_Close_Valve_36 := TRUE;
    FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS DO GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Enable[L_i] := FALSE; END_FOR;
    FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS DO GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pumps[L_i] := FALSE; END_FOR;
END_IF;

// 1. ЧТЕНИЕ И ФИЛЬТРАЦИЯ ВХОДОВ
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES DO
    fbDebounce_Switches[L_i](IN := GVL_IO.DI_Lighting_Switches[L_i], PT := L_Debounce_Time, VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS);
    GVL_STATE.G_Physical_Switches[L_i] := fbDebounce_Switches[L_i].Q;
    
    fbDebounce_Motion[L_i](IN := GVL_IO.DI_Motion_Sensors[L_i], PT := L_Debounce_Time, VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS);
    GVL_STATE.G_Motion_Sensors[L_i] := fbDebounce_Motion[L_i].Q;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SOCKETS DO
    fbDebounce_Socket_Switches[L_i](IN := GVL_IO.DI_Socket_Switches[L_i], PT := L_Debounce_Time, VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS);
    GVL_STATE.G_Socket_Switches[L_i] := fbDebounce_Socket_Switches[L_i].Q;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SECURITY_SENSORS DO
    fbDebounce_Security_Open[L_i](IN := GVL_IO.DI_Security_Open[L_i], PT := L_Debounce_Time, VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS);
    fbDebounce_Security_Glass[L_i](IN := GVL_IO.DI_Security_Glass[L_i], PT := L_Debounce_Time, VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS);
END_FOR;
fbDebounce_Group_2F(IN := GVL_IO.DI_Security_2F_Group, PT := L_Debounce_Time, VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS);

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_DOOR_SENSORS DO
    IF GVL_CONFIG.G_Door_Map[L_i] > 0 AND GVL_CONFIG.G_Door_Map[L_i] <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SECURITY_SENSORS THEN
        GVL_STATE.G_Door_Sensors[L_i] := fbDebounce_Security_Open[GVL_CONFIG.G_Door_Map[L_i]].Q;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES DO
    IF GVL_CONFIG.G_Window_Map[L_i] > 0 THEN
        IF GVL_CONFIG.G_Window_Map[L_i] <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SECURITY_SENSORS THEN
            GVL_STATE.G_Window_Sensors[L_i] := fbDebounce_Security_Open[GVL_CONFIG.G_Window_Map[L_i]].Q;
        ELSIF GVL_CONFIG.G_Window_Map[L_i] <= (GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SECURITY_SENSORS * 2) THEN
            GVL_STATE.G_Window_Sensors[L_i] := fbDebounce_Security_Glass[GVL_CONFIG.G_Window_Map[L_i] - GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SECURITY_SENSORS].Q;
        END_IF;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;
GVL_STATE.G_Window_Sensors[16] := fbDebounce_Group_2F.Q;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_FLOOD_SENSORS DO
    fbDebounce_Flood[L_i](IN := GVL_IO.DI_Flood_Sensors[L_i], PT := L_Debounce_Time, VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS);
    GVL_STATE.G_Water_Sensors[L_i] := fbDebounce_Flood[L_i].Q;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SMOKE_SENSORS DO
    fbDebounce_Smoke[L_i](IN := GVL_IO.DI_Smoke_Sensors[L_i], PT := L_Debounce_Time, VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS);
    GVL_STATE.G_Smoke_Sensors[L_i] := fbDebounce_Smoke[L_i].Q;
END_FOR;

IF GVL_IO.AI_Temp_Outdoor.wStatus = 0 THEN
    GVL_STATE.G_Outdoor_Temp := GVL_IO.AI_Temp_Outdoor.rValue;
END_IF;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_TEMPS DO
    IF GVL_IO.AI_Supply_Temps[L_i].wStatus = 0 THEN
        GVL_STATE.G_Supply_Temps[L_i] := GVL_IO.AI_Supply_Temps[L_i].rValue;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_HUMIDITY_SENSORS DO
    GVL_STATE.G_Room_Hum[L_i] := GVL_IO.AI_Room_Hum[L_i];
END_FOR;
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES DO
    GVL_STATE.G_Room_CO2[L_i] := GVL_IO.AI_Room_CO2[L_i];
END_FOR;
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES DO
    IF GVL_CONFIG.G_FloorTemp_Map[L_i] > 0 AND GVL_CONFIG.G_FloorTemp_Map[L_i] <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES THEN
        GVL_STATE.G_Floor_Temps[L_i] := GVL_IO.AI_Floor_Temps[GVL_CONFIG.G_FloorTemp_Map[L_i]];
    END_IF;
    IF GVL_CONFIG.G_RoomTemp_Map[L_i] > 0 AND GVL_CONFIG.G_RoomTemp_Map[L_i] <= GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES THEN
        GVL_STATE.G_Room_Temps[L_i] := GVL_IO.AI_Room_Temps[GVL_CONFIG.G_RoomTemp_Map[L_i]];
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS DO
    GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pressures[L_i] := INT_TO_REAL(GVL_IO.AI_Manifold_Pressures[L_i]) / 10.0;
    GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Currents[L_i] := INT_TO_REAL(GVL_IO.AI_Manifold_Currents[L_i]) / 100.0;
    IF GVL_IO.AI_Manifold_Temps_Supply[L_i].wStatus = 0 THEN
        GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_T_Supply[L_i] := GVL_IO.AI_Manifold_Temps_Supply[L_i].rValue;
    END_IF;
    GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_T_Return[L_i] := INT_TO_REAL(GVL_IO.AI_Manifold_Temps_Return[L_i]) / 10.0;
    GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_End_Switches[L_i] := GVL_IO.DI_Manifold_End_Switches[L_i];
END_FOR;

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_METHANE_SENSORS DO
    IF GVL_IO.AI_Methane_LEL[L_i].wStatus = 0 THEN
        GVL_STATE.G_Methane_Sensors[L_i] := GVL_IO.AI_Methane_LEL[L_i].rValue;
    END_IF;
END_FOR;
GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Flame := GVL_IO.AI_Boiler_Flame_Status;
GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Error := GVL_IO.DI_Boiler_Error;
GVL_STATE.G_CO_Sensors := GVL_IO.AI_CO_PPM;

GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Temp := GVL_IO.AI_DHW_Temp;
GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Pressure := GVL_IO.AI_DHW_Pressure;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
PROGRAM PRG_IO_Write
VAR
    L_i : INT;
    L_Lighting_Changed : BOOL;
    L_Blinds_Changed : BOOL;
    L_Prev_Lighting_Levels : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES] OF BYTE;
    L_Prev_Blinds_Positions : ARRAY[1..GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BLINDS] OF BYTE;
    fbInterfaceValidator : FB_Interface_Contract_Validator;
END_VAR

fbInterfaceValidator(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Enable := GVL_CONFIG.G_Hardware_Interface_Enable,
    VI_Strict_Mode := GVL_CONFIG.G_Hardware_Interface_Strict_Mode,
    VI_Manifold_Valves := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Valves,
    VI_Boiler_Setpoints := GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Setpoint,
    VI_Supply_Fans := GVL_STATE.G_Supply_Fans,
    VI_Exhaust_Fans := GVL_STATE.G_Exhaust_Fans,
    VI_Lighting_Levels := GVL_STATE.G_Lighting_Levels,
    VI_Blinds_Positions := GVL_STATE.G_Blinds_Positions,
    VI_DALI_Zone_Map := GVL_CONFIG.G_DALI_Zone_Map,
    VI_KNX_Blinds_Map := GVL_CONFIG.G_KNX_Blinds_Map,
    VO_Status => GVL_STATUS.G_Hardware_Interface_Status
);

// 2. ЗАПИСЬ ВЫХОДОВ (GVL_STATE -> GVL_IO)

// 2.1. Отопление (Термоэлектрические приводы)
GVL_IO.DO_Zone_Valves := GVL_STATE.G_Zone_Valves;

// 2.2. Коллекторы (Насосы и смесительные клапаны)
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS DO
    GVL_IO.DO_Manifold_Pumps[L_i] := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pumps[L_i];
    // Масштабирование 0.0-100.0% в 0-1000 для аналогового выхода (0-10В)
    GVL_IO.AO_Manifold_Valves[L_i] := REAL_TO_UINT(fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Manifold_Valves[L_i] * 10.0);
END_FOR;

// 2.3. Котлы
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS DO
    GVL_IO.DO_Boiler_Enable[L_i] := GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Enable[L_i];
    // Масштабирование уставки (например, 0-100 градусов в 0-1000 для 0-10В)
    GVL_IO.AO_Boiler_Setpoint[L_i] := REAL_TO_UINT(fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Boiler_Setpoints[L_i] * 10.0);
END_FOR;

// 2.4. Вентиляция
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SUPPLY_FANS DO
    GVL_IO.AO_Supply_Fans[L_i] := TO_UINT(fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Supply_Fans[L_i]) * 10;
END_FOR;
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_EXHAUST_FANS DO
    GVL_IO.AO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i] := TO_UINT(fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Exhaust_Fans[L_i]) * 10;
END_FOR;

// 2.5. ГВС
GVL_IO.DO_DHW_Heating_Pump := GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Heating_Pump;
GVL_IO.DO_DHW_Circ_Pump := GVL_STATE.G_DHW_Circ_Pump;

// 2.6. Освещение и шторы (контракт драйверного уровня для DALI/KNX шлюзов)
L_Lighting_Changed := FALSE;
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES DO
    GVL_GATEWAY.G_DALI_Lighting_Levels[L_i] := fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Lighting_Levels[L_i];
    IF fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Lighting_Levels[L_i] <> L_Prev_Lighting_Levels[L_i] THEN
        L_Lighting_Changed := TRUE;
        L_Prev_Lighting_Levels[L_i] := fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Lighting_Levels[L_i];
    END_IF;
END_FOR;
GVL_GATEWAY.G_DALI_Command_Update := L_Lighting_Changed;

L_Blinds_Changed := FALSE;
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BLINDS DO
    GVL_GATEWAY.G_KNX_Blinds_Positions[L_i] := fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Blinds_Positions[L_i];
    IF fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Blinds_Positions[L_i] <> L_Prev_Blinds_Positions[L_i] THEN
        L_Blinds_Changed := TRUE;
        L_Prev_Blinds_Positions[L_i] := fbInterfaceValidator.VO_Blinds_Positions[L_i];
    END_IF;
END_FOR;
GVL_GATEWAY.G_KNX_Command_Update := L_Blinds_Changed;

// 2.7. Аварийные выходы (Сирены и клапаны)
IF GVL_ALARM.G_Gas_Fire_Siren AND GVL_ALARM.G_Gas_Alarm_Active THEN
    GVL_IO.DO_Gas_Siren := TRUE;
ELSE
    GVL_IO.DO_Gas_Siren := FALSE;
END_IF;

IF GVL_ALARM.G_Gas_Fire_Siren AND GVL_ALARM.G_Fire_Alarm_Active THEN
    GVL_IO.DO_Fire_Siren := TRUE;
ELSE
    GVL_IO.DO_Fire_Siren := FALSE;
END_IF;

IF GVL_ALARM.G_Security_Siren THEN
    GVL_IO.DO_Security_Siren := TRUE;
ELSE
    GVL_IO.DO_Security_Siren := FALSE;
END_IF;

IF GVL_COMMAND.G_Close_Valve_35 THEN
    GVL_IO.DO_Water_Valve_35_Close := TRUE;
ELSE
    GVL_IO.DO_Water_Valve_35_Close := FALSE;
END_IF;

IF GVL_COMMAND.G_Close_Valve_36 THEN
    GVL_IO.DO_Water_Valve_36_Close := TRUE;
ELSE
    GVL_IO.DO_Water_Valve_36_Close := FALSE;
END_IF;

IF GVL_COMMAND.G_Gas_Valve_Close THEN
    GVL_IO.DO_Gas_Valve_Close := TRUE;
ELSE
    GVL_IO.DO_Gas_Valve_Close := FALSE;
END_IF;

// 2.8. Управление доступом (Периметральная автоматика)
GVL_IO.DO_Gate_Open := GVL_COMMAND.G_Gate_Open;
GVL_IO.DO_Wicket_Open := GVL_COMMAND.G_Wicket_Open;
GVL_IO.DO_Lock_1_Open := GVL_COMMAND.G_Lock_1_Open;
GVL_IO.DO_Lock_1_Close := GVL_COMMAND.G_Lock_1_Close;
GVL_IO.DO_Lock_2_Open := GVL_COMMAND.G_Lock_2_Open;
GVL_IO.DO_Lock_2_Close := GVL_COMMAND.G_Lock_2_Close;

// 2.9. Розетки
GVL_IO.DO_Sockets := GVL_STATE.G_Socket_States;

    VI_Flood_Alarm := GVL_ALARM.G_Flood_Alarm_Active,

    VO_Socket_States => GVL_STATE.G_Socket_States
);

PROGRAM PRG_System
VAR
    fbRedundancy : FB_Redundancy_Manager;
    fbGateway : FB_Gateway_Interface;
    fbScenarioManager : FB_Scenario_Manager;
    fbSimulationManager : FB_Simulation_Manager;
    fbRuleEngine : FB_Rule_Engine;
    fbNVRAMManager : FB_NVRAM_Manager;
    fbBlackBox : FB_BlackBox_Recorder;
    fbAstroTimer : FB_Astro_Timer;
    fbAlarmManager : FB_Alarm_Manager;
    fbHistoryManager : FB_History_Manager;
    fbDebugLogger : FB_Debug_Logger;
    fbOutdoorTrend : FB_Trend_Logger;
    fbMethaneTrend : FB_Trend_Logger;
    fbStateSnapshot : FB_State_Snapshot_Manager;
    fbSnapshotCRC : FB_CRC32_Calculator;
    
    L_Time_Diff : UDINT;
    L_Local_State : ST_System_State_Snapshot;
    L_Remote_State : ST_System_State_Snapshot;
    L_Config_Loaded : BOOL;
    L_NVRAM_Cmd : BYTE;
    L_NVRAM_Offset : UDINT;
    L_NVRAM_Done : BOOL;
    L_NVRAM_Err : BOOL;
    L_NVRAM_ErrID : UDINT;
    L_BB_Record : ST_BlackBox_Record;
    L_BB_Freeze : BOOL;
    L_Scenario_Idx : INT;
    L_i : INT;
    L_Diag_Error_Code : UDINT;
    L_Snapshot_Trigger : BOOL;
    L_Prev_Snapshot_Alarm : BOOL;
    L_Prev_Snapshot_Scenario : E_SCENARIO_TYPE;
    L_State_Snapshot : ST_State_Snapshot;
END_VAR

// 0. Инициализация RETAIN переменных при первом запуске
IF NOT GVL_Retain.G_Initialized THEN
    // Инициализация истории присутствия
    FOR L_i := 0 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_PRESENCE_HISTORY - 1 DO
        GVL_Retain.G_Presence_History[L_i] := 0;
    END_FOR;
    
    // Инициализация истории событий
    GVL_Retain.G_History_Write_Idx := 1;
    GVL_Retain.G_History_Total_Events := 0;
    
    // Инициализация статистики котлов
    FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_BOILERS DO
        GVL_Retain.G_Boiler_Accumulated_MS[L_i] := 0;
        GVL_Retain.G_Boiler_Work_Seconds[L_i] := 0;
    END_FOR;
    
    // Инициализация результатов тестирования клапанов
    FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_MANIFOLDS DO
        GVL_Retain.G_Valve_Test_Results[L_i] := FALSE;
    END_FOR;
    
    L_Local_State.Version := 0;
    L_Remote_State.Version := 0;
    
    GVL_Retain.G_Initialized := TRUE;
END_IF;

// 1. Обновление системного времени
GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS := TIME_TO_UDINT(TIME());
L_Time_Diff := F_TimeDiff(GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS, GVL_STATUS.G_Last_System_Time_MS);
GVL_STATUS.G_Time_Of_Day_MS := (GVL_STATUS.G_Time_Of_Day_MS + L_Time_Diff) MOD 86400000;

IF GVL_STATUS.G_Time_Of_Day_MS < L_Time_Diff THEN
    GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Day := (GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Day MOD 7) + 1;
    GVL_STATUS.G_Day_Of_Year := (GVL_STATUS.G_Day_Of_Year MOD 365) + 1;
END_IF;

GVL_STATUS.G_Last_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS;
GVL_STATUS.G_Current_TOD := UDINT_TO_TOD(GVL_STATUS.G_Time_Of_Day_MS);

// Формирование локального состояния для репликации
L_Local_State.System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS;
L_Local_State.Current_Scenario := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario;
L_Local_State.Security_Armed := GVL_ALARM.G_Security_Armed;
L_Local_State.Active_Alarms := GVL_ALARM.G_Active_Alarm_Count;
L_Local_State.Zone_Valves := GVL_STATE.G_Zone_Valves;
L_Local_State.Manifold_Pumps := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pumps;
L_Local_State.Boiler_Enable := GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Enable;
L_Local_State.Lighting_States := GVL_STATE.G_Lighting_Levels;
L_Local_State.Blinds_Positions := GVL_STATE.G_Blinds_Positions;
L_Local_State.Socket_States := GVL_STATE.G_Socket_States;
L_Local_State.Gas_Valve_Closed := GVL_COMMAND.G_Gas_Valve_Close;
L_Local_State.Water_Valves_Closed := GVL_COMMAND.G_Close_Valve_36;
L_Local_State.Version := L_Local_State.Version + 1;

// 2. Определение роли ПЛК (Active/Standby)
fbRedundancy(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Local_PLC_ID := GVL_STATUS.G_PLC_ID,
    VI_Remote_Pulse := GVL_IO.DI_Partner_Pulse,
    VI_Remote_Is_Active := GVL_IO.DI_Partner_Active,
    VI_Gateway_Ping_OK := GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Ping_OK,
    VI_Local_State := L_Local_State,
    VI_Remote_State := L_Remote_State
);
GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC := (fbRedundancy.VO_Local_Role = E_PLC_ROLE.ROLE_ACTIVE);
GVL_IO.DO_Heartbeat_Pulse := fbRedundancy.VO_Local_Pulse;
GVL_IO.DO_Active_Status := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC;

// 3. Синхронизация состояния (применение полученного состояния)
IF fbRedundancy.VO_State_Updated THEN
    GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Current_Scenario;
    GVL_ALARM.G_Security_Armed := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Security_Armed;
    GVL_STATE.G_Zone_Valves := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Zone_Valves;
    GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pumps := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Manifold_Pumps;
    GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Enable := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Boiler_Enable;
    GVL_STATE.G_Lighting_Levels := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Lighting_States;
    GVL_STATE.G_Blinds_Positions := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Blinds_Positions;
    GVL_STATE.G_Socket_States := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Socket_States;
    GVL_COMMAND.G_Gas_Valve_Close := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Gas_Valve_Closed;
    GVL_COMMAND.G_Close_Valve_36 := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Water_Valves_Closed;
    L_Local_State.Version := fbRedundancy.VO_Synced_State.Version;
END_IF;

// 4. Астрономический таймер
fbAstroTimer(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Current_TOD := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_TOD,
    VI_Latitude := 55.75,
    VI_Longitude := 37.61,
    VI_Day_Of_Year := GVL_STATUS.G_Day_Of_Year,
    VO_Is_Night => GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Night
);

// 5. Управление сценариями
fbScenarioManager(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Activate_Request := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario,
    VI_IsActivePLC := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC,
    VO_Current_Scenario => GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario
);

L_Scenario_Idx := TO_INT(GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario);
IF L_Scenario_Idx < 1 OR L_Scenario_Idx > GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_SCENARIOS THEN
    L_Scenario_Idx := 1;
END_IF;

// 6. Симуляция присутствия
fbSimulationManager(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_IsActivePLC := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC,
    VI_Scenario := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario,
    VI_Config := GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Scenario_Configs[L_Scenario_Idx],
    VO_Sim_Lights => GVL_STATE.G_Sim_Lights,
    VO_Sim_Active => GVL_STATUS.G_Sim_Active
);

// 6.5. Пользовательские правила (Rule Engine)
fbRuleEngine(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_IsActivePLC := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC,
    VI_Rules := GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_User_Rules,
    VI_Indoor_Temps := GVL_STATE.G_Room_Temps,
    VI_Floor_Temps := GVL_STATE.G_Floor_Temps,
    VI_Humidities := GVL_STATE.G_Room_Hum,
    VI_CO2_Levels := GVL_STATE.G_Room_CO2,
    VI_Motion_Sensors := GVL_STATE.G_Motion_Sensors,
    VI_Door_Sensors := GVL_STATE.G_Door_Sensors,
    VI_Window_Sensors := GVL_STATE.G_Window_Sensors,
    VI_Water_Sensors := GVL_STATE.G_Water_Sensors,
    VI_Smoke_Sensors := GVL_STATE.G_Smoke_Sensors,
    VI_Methane_Sensors := GVL_STATE.G_Methane_Sensors,
    VI_CO_Sensors := GVL_STATE.G_CO_Sensors,
    VI_Security_Armed := GVL_ALARM.G_Security_Armed,
    VI_Current_Time := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_TOD,
    VI_Day_Of_Week := TO_INT(GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Day),
    VO_Actions => GVL_STATE.G_Rule_Actions
);

FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_RULES DO
    IF GVL_STATE.G_Rule_Actions[L_i].Active AND GVL_STATE.G_Rule_Actions[L_i].Action_Type = E_Rule_Action_Type.ACTION_ACTIVATE_SCENARIO THEN
        GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario := TO_BYTE(GVL_STATE.G_Rule_Actions[L_i].Value);
    END_IF;
END_FOR;

// 8.5 Менеджер тревог (Сбор всех аварий)
fbAlarmManager(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_IsActivePLC := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC,
    VI_Gas_Alarm := GVL_ALARM.G_Gas_Alarm_Active,
    VI_Fire_Alarm := GVL_ALARM.G_Fire_Alarm_Active,
    VI_Flood_Alarm := GVL_ALARM.G_Flood_Alarm_Active,
    VI_Security_Alarm := GVL_ALARM.G_Security_Alarm,
    VI_Boiler_Errors := GVL_STATE.G_Boiler_Error,
    VI_Security_Msg := GVL_STATUS.G_Security_Status_Msg,
    VI_Acknowledge_All := GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Ack_Alarms OR GVL_COMMAND.G_Reset_Errors,
    VI_Mute_Siren := GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Mute_Alarm,
    VIO_Next_Alarm_ID := GVL_ALARM.G_Next_Alarm_ID,
    VO_Global_Critical => GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Critical,
    VO_Global_Warning => GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Warning,
    VO_Siren_Active => GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Siren,
    VO_Active_Count => GVL_ALARM.G_Active_Alarm_Count,
    VO_Unacked_Count => GVL_ALARM.G_Unacked_Alarm_Count,
    VO_Alarm_List => GVL_ALARM.G_Alarm_List
);

// 9.0 Служебная диагностика и сервисные блоки Stage 1
IF L_NVRAM_Err THEN
    L_Diag_Error_Code := L_NVRAM_ErrID;
ELSIF GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Critical THEN
    L_Diag_Error_Code := 16#E100;
ELSIF GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Warning THEN
    L_Diag_Error_Code := 16#E010;
ELSE
    L_Diag_Error_Code := 0;
END_IF;

fbDebugLogger(
    VI_Config := (enabled := TRUE, sampling_period_ms := GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MS_IN_MINUTE),
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Floor_Temps := GVL_STATE.G_Floor_Temps,
    VI_Pump_Currents := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Currents,
    VI_Error_Code := L_Diag_Error_Code
);

fbOutdoorTrend(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Config := (param_type := TO_BYTE(E_Trend_Parameter_Type.TREND_PARAM_TEMP_AIR), zone_id := 0, enabled := TRUE, deviation_threshold_percent := 5.0, history_days := 7),
    VI_Current_Value := GVL_STATE.G_Outdoor_Temp
);

fbMethaneTrend(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Config := (param_type := TO_BYTE(E_Trend_Parameter_Type.TREND_PARAM_GAS_METHANE), zone_id := 1, enabled := TRUE, deviation_threshold_percent := 5.0, history_days := 7),
    VI_Current_Value := GVL_STATE.G_Methane_Sensors[1]
);

L_Snapshot_Trigger := (GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Critical AND NOT L_Prev_Snapshot_Alarm) OR (GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario <> L_Prev_Snapshot_Scenario);
L_State_Snapshot.timestamp_ms := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS;
L_State_Snapshot.operator_id := 'SYSTEM';
L_State_Snapshot.scenario_id := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario;
L_State_Snapshot.lighting_levels := GVL_STATE.G_Lighting_Levels;
FOR L_i := 1 TO GVL_CONSTANTS.C_MAX_ZONES DO
    L_State_Snapshot.floor_heating_setpoints[L_i] := GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_FloorHeating_Configs[L_i].design_temp;
END_FOR;
L_State_Snapshot.alarm_active := GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Critical OR GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Warning;
L_State_Snapshot.crc32 := 0;
L_State_Snapshot.crc32 := fbSnapshotCRC.Calculate(ADR(L_State_Snapshot), SIZEOF(L_State_Snapshot) - SIZEOF(L_State_Snapshot.crc32));

fbStateSnapshot(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Trigger_Event := L_Snapshot_Trigger,
    VI_Event_Code := SEL(GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Critical, 1001, 9001),
    VI_Current_State := L_State_Snapshot
);
L_Prev_Snapshot_Alarm := GVL_ALARM.G_Global_Critical;
L_Prev_Snapshot_Scenario := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario;

// 13. Интерфейс шлюза (Modbus TCP)
fbGateway(
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Local_PLC_Role := SEL(GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC, E_PLC_ROLE.ROLE_STANDBY, E_PLC_ROLE.ROLE_ACTIVE),
    VI_Incoming_Command := GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Command,
    VI_Command_Received := GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Command_Received,
    VI_FloorHeating_Temps := GVL_STATE.G_Floor_Temps,
    VI_Room_Temps := GVL_STATE.G_Room_Temps,
    VI_Zone_Valve_States := GVL_STATE.G_Zone_Valves,
    VI_Manifold_Pressures := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pressures,
    VI_Manifold_Pump_States := GVL_STATE.G_Manifold_Pumps,
    VI_Outdoor_Temp := GVL_STATE.G_Outdoor_Temp,
    VI_Security_Armed := GVL_ALARM.G_Security_Armed,
    VI_Flood_Alarm_Active := GVL_ALARM.G_Flood_Alarm_Active,
    VI_Gas_Alarm_Active := GVL_ALARM.G_Gas_Alarm_Active,
    VI_Fire_Alarm_Active := GVL_ALARM.G_Fire_Alarm_Active,
    VI_Methane_Concentration := GVL_STATE.G_Methane_Sensors[1],
    VI_Lighting_Base_Levels := GVL_STATE.G_Lighting_Levels,
    VI_Socket_States := GVL_STATE.G_Socket_States,
    VI_Blinds_Positions := GVL_STATE.G_Blinds_Positions,
    VI_Active_Scenario := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario,
    VI_Send_2FA_Req := GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Send_2FA,
    VI_2FA_Code := GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_2FA_Code,
    VI_Allowed_IPs := GVL_CONFIG.G_Allowed_IPs,
    VO_Telegram_Msg => GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Telegram_Msg,
    VO_Send_Telegram => GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Send_Telegram,
    VO_HMI_Status_Message => GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_HMI_Status_Message,
    VO_Ping_OK => GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Ping_OK,
    VO_Data_Ready => GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Data_Ready,
    VO_Modbus_Registers => GVL_GATEWAY.G_Gateway_Modbus_Registers,
    VO_Arm_Req => GVL_COMMAND.G_Arm_Req,
    VO_Disarm_Req => GVL_COMMAND.G_Disarm_Req,
    VO_PIN_Code => GVL_COMMAND.G_PIN_Code,
    VO_RFID_Tag => GVL_COMMAND.G_RFID_Tag,
    VO_2FA_Code_In => GVL_COMMAND.G_2FA_Code_In,
    VO_Lighting_Override => GVL_COMMAND.G_Lighting_Override,
    VO_Blinds_Override => GVL_COMMAND.G_Blinds_Override,
    VO_Socket_Override => GVL_COMMAND.G_Socket_Override,
    VO_Reset_Errors_Req => GVL_COMMAND.G_Reset_Errors
);

IF fbGateway.VO_Set_Scenario_Req THEN
    GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario := fbGateway.VO_Target_Scenario;
END_IF;

IF fbGateway.VO_Set_Temp_Req THEN
    GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_FloorHeating_Configs[fbGateway.VO_Target_Zone].design_temp := fbGateway.VO_Target_Temp;
END_IF;

IF fbGateway.VO_Set_Vent_Req THEN
    GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Vent_Global_Config.default_supply_speed := fbGateway.VO_Target_Vent_Speed;
END_IF;

IF fbGateway.VO_Set_Config_Req THEN
    GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Apply_Settings := TRUE;
END_IF;

IF fbGateway.VO_Sync_Time_Req THEN
    GVL_STATUS.G_Time_Of_Day_MS := fbGateway.VO_New_Time_MS;
END_IF;

// 14. Менеджер NVRAM
IF NOT L_Config_Loaded THEN
    L_NVRAM_Cmd := 2; // READ
    L_NVRAM_Offset := 0;
    L_Config_Loaded := TRUE;
ELSIF GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Apply_Settings THEN
    L_NVRAM_Cmd := 1; // WRITE
    L_NVRAM_Offset := 0;
    GVL_CONFIG.G_HMI_Apply_Settings := FALSE;
ELSE
    L_NVRAM_Cmd := 0;
END_IF;

fbNVRAMManager(
    VI_Command := L_NVRAM_Cmd,
    VI_Offset := L_NVRAM_Offset,
    VI_DataPtr := ADR(GVL_CONFIG),
    VI_DataSize := SIZEOF(GVL_CONFIG),
    VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
    VI_Operator_ID := 'SYSTEM',
    VI_IsActivePLC := GVL_STATUS.G_Is_Active_PLC,
    VI_TwoPersonConfirmation := FALSE,
    VO_Done => L_NVRAM_Done,
    VO_Error => L_NVRAM_Err,
    VO_ErrorID => L_NVRAM_ErrID
);

// 15. Черный ящик
L_BB_Record.Timestamp := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS;
L_BB_Record.PLC_Active_ID := GVL_STATUS.G_PLC_ID;
L_BB_Record.Gas_Methane_LEL := GVL_STATE.G_Methane_Sensors[1];
L_BB_Record.Gas_CO_PPM := GVL_STATE.G_CO_Sensors[1];
L_BB_Record.Flood_Active := GVL_ALARM.G_Flood_Alarm_Active;
L_BB_Record.Fire_Active := GVL_ALARM.G_Fire_Alarm_Active;
L_BB_Record.Valve_Gas_Status := TO_BYTE(SEL(GVL_COMMAND.G_Gas_Valve_Close, 1, 0));
L_BB_Record.Valve_Water_Status := TO_BYTE(SEL(GVL_COMMAND.G_Close_Valve_35 OR GVL_COMMAND.G_Close_Valve_36, 1, 0));

L_BB_Freeze := GVL_ALARM.G_Gas_Alarm_Active OR GVL_ALARM.G_Fire_Alarm_Active OR GVL_ALARM.G_Flood_Alarm_Active;

fbBlackBox(
    VI_Current_Data := L_BB_Record,
    VI_Freeze := L_BB_Freeze
);

// 15.1. Менеджер истории
IF GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario <> GVL_STATUS.G_Previous_Scenario THEN
    fbHistoryManager(
        VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS,
        VI_Write_Event := TRUE,
        VI_Event := (timestamp_ms := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS, event_code := 1001, event_value := TO_REAL(GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario), unit := 0, zone_id := 0, operator_id := 'SYSTEM', priority := E_ALERT_PRIORITY.ALERT_PRIORITY_LOW)
    );
    GVL_STATUS.G_Previous_Scenario := GVL_STATUS.G_Current_Scenario;
ELSE
    fbHistoryManager(VI_System_Time_MS := GVL_STATUS.G_System_Time_MS, VI_Write_Event := FALSE);
END_IF;

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
PROGRAM PRG_Test
VAR
    // Инстансы тестируемых блоков
    fbAnalogValidator : FB_Analog_Validator;
    fbRandomGenerator : FB_Random_Generator;
    fbTwoFactorAuth   : FB_TwoFactor_Auth;
    
    // Переменные для тестов
    L_Test_Step : INT := 0;
    L_Tests_Passed : INT := 0;
    L_Tests_Failed : INT := 0;
    L_System_Time : UDINT := 0;
    
    // Результаты тестов
    L_Test1_Passed : BOOL;
    L_Test2_Passed : BOOL;
    L_Test3_Passed : BOOL;
    L_Random_Value : UDINT;
END_VAR

// Имитация системного времени
L_System_Time := L_System_Time + 10;

CASE L_Test_Step OF
    0: // Инициализация
        L_Test_Step := 1;
        
    1: // Тест 1: FB_Analog_Validator - Нормальное значение
        fbAnalogValidator(
            VI_Value := 25.0,
            VI_Min_Valid := 0.0,
            VI_Max_Valid := 50.0,
            VI_Fallback_Mode := 0,
            VI_Default_Value := 20.0
        );
        IF NOT fbAnalogValidator.VO_Error AND fbAnalogValidator.VO_Value = 25.0 THEN
            L_Test1_Passed := TRUE;
            L_Tests_Passed := L_Tests_Passed + 1;
        ELSE
            L_Test1_Passed := FALSE;
            L_Tests_Failed := L_Tests_Failed + 1;
        END_IF;
        L_Test_Step := 2;
        
    2: // Тест 2: FB_Analog_Validator - Выход за границы (Fallback = Default)
        fbAnalogValidator(
            VI_Value := 100.0,
            VI_Min_Valid := 0.0,
            VI_Max_Valid := 50.0,
            VI_Fallback_Mode := 1,
            VI_Default_Value := 20.0
        );
        IF fbAnalogValidator.VO_Error AND fbAnalogValidator.VO_Value = 20.0 THEN
            L_Test2_Passed := TRUE;
            L_Tests_Passed := L_Tests_Passed + 1;
        ELSE
            L_Test2_Passed := FALSE;
            L_Tests_Failed := L_Tests_Failed + 1;
        END_IF;
        L_Test_Step := 3;
        
    3: // Тест 3: FB_Random_Generator - Диапазон
        fbRandomGenerator.Seed(VI_Seed_Value := 12345);
        L_Random_Value := fbRandomGenerator.Random_Int_Range(VI_min := 10, VI_max := 20, VI_System_Time_MS := L_System_Time);
        IF L_Random_Value >= 10 AND L_Random_Value <= 20 THEN
            L_Test3_Passed := TRUE;
            L_Tests_Passed := L_Tests_Passed + 1;
        ELSE
            L_Test3_Passed := FALSE;
            L_Tests_Failed := L_Tests_Failed + 1;
        END_IF;
        L_Test_Step := 100; // Завершение тестов
        
    100: // Тесты завершены
        // Здесь можно вывести результаты в лог или HMI
        ;
END_CASE;
